 The festival of Gangaur is celebrated on Chaitra Shukla Tritiya, also known as Gauri Tritiya
 holi ke duusare din (caitra krishna pratipada) se jo kumari or vivaahit or navvivaahit mahilaayein pratidin gangaur puujati hai or caitra shukla dwitiya (sinjaare) ke din kisi nadi, talab yaa sarovar par jaakar apni puji hui ganagauron ko pani pilaati hai
 After this, immerse them in the evening on the second day
 yah vrath vivaahit mahilaayein pati kaa pyaar or sneh paane ke liye karti hai
 By observing this fast, the girls of Kuwari get a good husband and the suhaag of the Suhagins remains unbroken
 kya he gangaur vrath kii kathaek baar bhagwaan shankar tathaa parvatiji naradji ke saath bhraman ko nikle
 While walking, they reached a village on the day of Chaitra Shukla Tritiya
 unke aagaman kaa samachar sunakar gaanv kii shreshth kuleen striyaan unke swaagat ke liye swaadisht bhojan banane lageen
 They were very late while preparing food
 kintu saadhaaran kul kii striyaan shreshth kul kii striyon se pehle hi thaaliyon main haldi tathaa akshat lekar pujan hetu pahunch gayi
 Parvatiji accepted his worship spirit and sprinkled the whole honeymoon on him
 ve atal suhaag prapti kaa vardaan paakar lautin

 sone-chaandi se nirmit unki thaaliyon main vibhinn prakaar ke padaarth the
 Seeing those women, Lord Shankar said to Parvatiji - 'you gave all the suhaag juice to the women of the ordinary family
 ab inhen kya dogi?'parvatiji ne uttar diya- 'prannath! aap isaki chintaa mat kiijie
 i have given those women only juice made from upper substances
 isliye unka ras dhoti se rahegaa
 But i will rip my finger off these high clan women and give them a pleasant taste of blood
 yah suhaag ras jiske bhagya main padegaa, vah tan-man se mujh jaisi saubhagyawati ho jaaegi
 'when the women finished the worship, Parvatiji ripped his finger and sprinkled it on them
 jis par jaisaa chhinta padaa, usne vaisaa hi suhaag paa liya
 After this, with the permission of Lord Shiva, Parvatiji took a bath on the river bank and started worshiping after making a Shiva idol of sand
 pujan ke baad baaluu ke pakwaan banaakar shivaji ko bhoga lagaaya

 parantu mahadev to mahadev hi the

 After eating it, i am coming straight here
 ' yah sunakar shivaji bhi doodh-bhaat khaane kii laalach main nadi-tat kii ore chal die
 Parvati was confused
 tab unhone maun bhav se bhagwaan bhole shankar kaa hi dhyaan kiya or prarthana kii - he bhagwan! yadi main aapaki anany daasi hum to aap is samay meri laaj rakhie

 unhen dur nadi ke tat par maaya kaa mahal dikhaai diya

 tisare din parvatiji ne shiv se chalane ke liye kaha, par shivaji taiyaar na hue
 They wanted to stay still
 tab parvatiji ruuthakar akeli hi chal deen
 In such a situation Lord Shiva had to walk with Parvati
 naradji bhi saath-saath chal die
 While walking, they came out very far
 us samay bhagwaan surya apane dham (pashchim) ko padhaar rahe the

 How to fast Gangaur- Bathing on Ekadashi of Chaitra Krishna Paksha in the morning should be done in wet clothes and sow jowar in a wooden basket in a sacred place of the house
 - is din se visarjan tak vrati ko ekasana (ek samay bhojan) rakhana chahie
 - These jwars are considered to be the form of Goddess Gauri and Shiva or Isar
 - jab tak gauriji kaa visarjan nahin ho jaataa (kareeb aath din) tab tak pratidin donon samay gauriji kii vidhi-vidhaan se puja kar unhen bhoga lagaana chahie
 - Gauri, Uma, Latika, Subhaga, Bhagmalini, Manokamna, Bhavani, Kamada, Bhoga Verdwini and Ambik
 maa gauri ke sabhi rupon kii purna shraddha or vishwaas se puja kerani chahie
 - Women who observe this fast should do this fast by drinking milk only once a day
 - gauriji kii is sthapana par suhaag kii vasteen jaise kaanch kii chudiyaan, sindur, mahavar, mehandi, tikaa, bindi, kanghee, sheesha, kaajal aadi chadhaai jaati hai
 - Suhag material is worshiped methodically with sandalwood, akshat, incense-lamp, naivedyadi and offered to Gauri
 - iske pashchaat gauriji ko bhoga lagaaya jaataa he or bhoga ke baad gauriji kii katha kahi jaati he

 - caitra shukla dwitiya (sinjaare) ko gauriji ko kisi nadi, talab yaa sarovar par le jaakar unhen snaan karaaen

 - isi din shaam ko ek shobhaayatra ke rup main gauri-shiv ko nadi, talab yaa sarovar par le jaakar visarjeet karen
 - Fasting is also opened in the evening on the same day after immersion
 - pujan main maa gauri ke das rupon kii puja kii jaati he
